        LEFT OUTER JOIN  (SELECT [Extent2].[AdminUserId] AS [AdminUserId], [Extent3].[Id] AS [Id], [Extent3].[Name] AS [Name], [Extent3].[CreateDateTime] AS [CreateDateTime], [Extent3].[IsDeleted] AS [IsDeleted]
